    4486              : /**
    4487              :  * @brief Handles special case when loading INT4 data with unaligned src_stride
    4488              :  * 
    4489              :  * When processing INT4 data and (i * src_stride_) % 2 != 0, we need to perform additional operations
    4490              :  * to handle the unaligned half-byte boundaries:
    4491              :  * 
    4492              :  * - For small loads (< 8 bytes or tail cases): We perform a simple right shift by 4 bits
    4493              :  *   to eliminate the unnecessary half-byte at the front
    4494              :  * 
    4495              :  * - For large loads (8 bytes): We need two registers to correctly reconstruct the data:
    4496              :  *   1. Shift the first register right by 4 bits to remove leading half-byte
    4497              :  *   2. Shift the second register left by 4 bits to preserve trailing half-byte
    4498              :  *   3. Combine both registers with logical OR to get the correctly aligned result
    4499              :  * 
    4500              :  * @param xmm_in The target XMM register to store the aligned data
    4501              :  * @param i Current row index
    4502              :  * @param columns_tail Number of remaining columns in the tail case
    4503              :  * @param is_tail Flag indicating if processing a tail section
    4504              :  * @param offset Memory offset for loading from source
    4505              :  * @return True if INT4 preloading was performed, false otherwise
    4506              :  */
    4507              : template <typename Vmm>
